# Hwarang spiritual guidance events

namespace = soh

##### Spiritual Guidance

### Seek spiritual guidance - approach possible religious person

# Someone asks you for spiritual guidance - do you accept?
character_event = {
	id = soh.1001
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1001
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # ask_for_spiritual_guidance targeted_decision
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1001 # Sure!
		
		piety = 25
		
		FROMFROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1002 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROMFROM
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					is_rival = FROMFROM
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				any_friend = {
					character = FROMFROM
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				any_lover = {
					character = FROMFROM
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				trait = greedy
			}
			religion = FROMFROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1001 # Make a donation to charity and I'll do it!
		
		piety = 15
		
		FROMFROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1003 } # Inform FROMFROM
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				is_rival = FROMFROM
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					trait = charitable
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = {
					trait = kind
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = {
					trait = content
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			trait = greedy
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_1001 # Pay me and I'll do it!
		
		piety = -25
		
		FROMFROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1006 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROMFROM
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				is_rival = FROMFROM
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = kind
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = content
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_landed = yes
				has_dlc = "Conclave"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_dlc = "Conclave"
			NOR = {
				owes_favor_to = FROMFROM
				holds_favor_on = FROMFROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_1001 # Give me a Favor and I'll do it!
		
		piety = -25
		
		FROMFROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1009 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROMFROM
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10 # Getting a Favor is good!
				is_rival = FROMFROM
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = content
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = ambitious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				is_landed = no
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NAND = {
					is_voter = yes
					liege = {
						character = FROMFROM
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_dlc = "Conclave"
			owes_favor_to = FROMFROM
		}
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_1001 # Consider it repayment of the Favor and I'll do it!
		
		piety = -25
		
		FROMFROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1012 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROMFROM
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				is_rival = FROMFROM
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = content
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = ambitious
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				is_landed = no
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NAND = {
					is_voter = yes
					liege = {
						character = FROMFROM
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_1001 # Not happening!
		
		piety = -50
		
		# GRACETODO
		
		FROMFROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1015 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROMFROM
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_friend = FROMFROM
					is_lover = FROMFROM
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 100
				any_rival = {
					character = FROMFROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Request accepted
character_event = {
	id = soh.1002
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1002
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1002 # Just what I wanted to hear!
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_hwarang_spiritual_guidance
			}
			
			clr_quest = {
				id = quest_hwarang_spiritual_guidance
			}
			
			add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1016 days = 30 random = 30 } # Lesson selection
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_hwarang_offering_spiritual_guidance
		}
		
		reverse_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_hwarang_receiving_spiritual_guidance
		}
	}
}

# Religious person requests charity
character_event = {
	id = soh.1003
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1003
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1003 # That sounds fair!
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_hwarang_spiritual_guidance
			}
			
			clr_quest = {
				id = quest_hwarang_spiritual_guidance
			}
			
			add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1004 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROM
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1016 days = 30 random = 30 } # Lesson selection
		}
		
		scaled_wealth = {
			value = -1
			min = -100
			max = -1000
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_hwarang_offering_spiritual_guidance
		}
		
		reverse_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_hwarang_receiving_spiritual_guidance
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = charitable
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				trait = greedy
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1003 # Charity? Such nonsense!
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1005 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROM
		}
		
		piety = -25
		
		remove_trait_charitable_effect = yes
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = greedy
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				trait = charitable
			}
		}
	}
}

# Religious person requests Favor
character_event = {
	id = soh.1009
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1009
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1009 # That sounds fair!
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_hwarang_spiritual_guidance
			}
			
			clr_quest = {
				id = quest_hwarang_spiritual_guidance
			}
			
			add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1010 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROM
			
			character_event = { id = soh.1016 days = 30 random = 30 } # Lesson selection
			
			add_favor = ROOT
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_hwarang_offering_spiritual_guidance
		}
		
		reverse_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_hwarang_receiving_spiritual_guidance
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			
			trigger = {
				NAND = {
					is_rival = FROMs
					NOT = {
						trait = trusting
					}
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = trusting
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = content
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				trait = paranoid
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				FROM = {
					is_landed = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1009 # A Favor? Never!
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1011 days = 1 random = 2 } # Inform FROM
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 100
				trait = paranoid
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
	}
}

### Seek spiritual guidance - guidance setup

# Hidden event to select something for religious person to try to teach
character_event = {
	id = soh.1016
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		# Clear all flags first
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_chaste
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_temperate
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_charitable
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_diligent
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_patient
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_kind
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_humble
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_brave
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_content
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_gregarious
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_honest
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_just
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_trusting
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_zealous
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_lustful
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_gluttonous
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_greedy
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_slothful
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_wroth
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_envious
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_proud
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_arbitrary
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_craven
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_cruel
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_cynical
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_deceitful
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_paranoid
		clr_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_shy
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			# First pick a good trait we have and could teach
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						OR = {
							trait = chaste
							trait = celibate
						}
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = chaste
							}
						}
						
						NAND = {
							any_lover = {
								character = FROM
							}
							NOR = {
								any_spouse = {
									character = FROM
								}
								any_consort = {
									character = FROM
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_chaste
				}
				
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						trait = temperate
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = temperate
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_temperate
				}
				
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						trait = charitable
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = charitable
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_charitable
				}
				
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						trait = diligent
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_diligent
				}
				
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						trait = patient
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = patient
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_character_flag = hwarang_spiritual_guidance_patient
				}
				
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						trait = kind
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = kind
							}
						}

### Spiritual guidance - chastity

# Inform Hwarang that they'll be taught about chastity
character_event = {
	id = soh.1018
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1018
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1018 # Sounds fair!
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1019 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to teacher
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1019
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}

			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1019 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again

	}
}

# I have a lover - maybe break up with them?
character_event = {
	id = soh.1020
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1020
	picture = GFX_evt_lovers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_lover = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					any_spouse = {
						character = ROOT
					}
					any_consort = {
						character = ROOT
					}
					character = FROM
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = breakup_target
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1020 # It is for the best...
		
		remove_lover = event_target:breakup_target
		
		event_target:breakup_target = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1021 } # Inform the lover
		}
		
		piety = 10
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1022 } # Inform teacher of progress
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1019 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = lustful
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1020 # No, I can't do that...
		
		piety = -10
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1023 } # Inform teacher of lack of progress
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1019 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = stubborn
			}
		}
	}
}

				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1036 # That's it! This ends now!

		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_friend = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_rival = ROOT
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			
			character_event = { id = soh.1038 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = diligent
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = humble
			}
		}
	}
}

# Approached by an attractive servant with appropriate gender and orientation - how dedicated are you to this chastity thing?
character_event = {
	id = soh.1041
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1041
	picture = GFX_evt_dancing
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				NOT = {
					trait = homosexual
				}
			}
			
			create_character = {
				female = yes
				dynasty = none
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				trait = underhanded_rogue
				trait = lustful
				trait = attractive
				random_traits = no
			}
			
			new_character = {
				save_event_target_as = tempting_servant
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				NOT = {
					trait = homosexual
				}
			}
			
			create_character = {
				female = no
				dynasty = none
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				trait = underhanded_rogue
				trait = lustful
				trait = attractive
				random_traits = no
			}
			
			new_character = {
				save_event_target_as = tempting_servant
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				trait = homosexual
			}
			
			create_character = {
				female = no
				dynasty = none
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				trait = underhanded_rogue
				trait = lustful
				trait = attractive
				trait = homosexual
				random_traits = no
			}
			
			new_character = {
				save_event_target_as = tempting_servant
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				trait = homosexual
			}
			
			create_character = {
				female = yes
				dynasty = none
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				trait = underhanded_rogue
				trait = lustful
				trait = attractive
				trait = homosexual
				random_traits = no
			}
			
			new_character = {
				save_event_target_as = tempting_servant
			}
		}
		
		event_target:tempting_servant = {
			remove_trait = celibate
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1041 # The flesh is weak...
		
		add_trait_lustful_effect = yes
		
		piety = -25
		
		event_target:tempting_servant = {
			save_event_target_as = sex_partner
			add_lover = ROOT
		}
		
		unprotected_sex_effect_event_target = yes
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1042 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1019 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					trait = celibate
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1041 # I'm better than this!
		
		piety = 10
		
		event_target:tempting_servant = {
			leave_court_and_die_effect = yes
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1019 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = cynical
			}
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1051
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								trait = gluttonous
								trait = drunkard
							}
						}
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = temperate
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Gluttonous or a Drunkard and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1052 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = temperate
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = temperate
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1057 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = temperate
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1063 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = gluttonous
								trait = drunkard
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Temperate
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1065 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = temperate
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1067 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = temperate
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1051 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1051 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

						any_friend = {

						}

			}

				remove_friend = ROOT
			}

		}

				trait = cynical

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1072
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = greedy
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Greedy and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1073 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						trait = charitable
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = charitable
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Suggest a charitable donation
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1077 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						trait = greedy
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = charitable
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Suggest giving money to teacher
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1083 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = charitable
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = charitable
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1090 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = charitable
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1096 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = greedy
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Charitable
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1098 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = charitable
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1100 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = charitable
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1072 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1072 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = slothful
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cynical
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 5
					trait = stubborn
				}

					factor = 5

		}

			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}

			}

		}

			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1105
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Slothful and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1106 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Diligence is hard work
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1110 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = diligent
								trait = stressed
							}
						}
					}

					# FROM becomes Stressed
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1112 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = diligent
								trait = wroth
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes less patient
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1114 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = diligent
								trait = ambitious
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes less content
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1117 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = diligent
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1120 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1126 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = slothful
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Diligent
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1128 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1130 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1105 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1105 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

			}

				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1123 # Let's keep at it...
		
		prestige = -25
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1105 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = slothful
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1123 # That's it! This ends now!
		
		piety = -10
		
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_friend = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_rival = ROOT
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			
			character_event = { id = soh.1125 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = diligent
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = humble
			}
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1135
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = wroth
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Wroth and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1136 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = patient
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Patience takes forever
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1140 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = patient
								trait = slothful
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes less diligent
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1142 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = patient
								trait = content
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes less ambitious
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1145 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = patient
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = patient
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1148 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = patient
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1154 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = wroth
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Patient
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1156 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = patient
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1158 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = patient
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1135 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1135 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# I am Wroth and am having second thoughts
character_event = {
	id = soh.1136
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1136
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1136 # It is for the best...
		
		piety = 10
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = diligent
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = zealous
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
				}
				
				remove_trait_wroth_effect = yes
				
				FROM = {
					character_event = { id = soh.1137 } # Inform teacher
				}
			}
			
			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = slothful
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cynical
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 5
					trait = stubborn
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 5
					trait = proud
				}
				
				FROM = {
					character_event = { id = soh.1138 } # Inform teacher
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1135 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = patient
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1136 # No, I can't do this...
		
		piety = -10
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1139 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}
}

				NOT = {
					trait = proud
				}
			}

				factor = 0.1
				trait = wroth
			}

				factor = 0.1
				trait = slothful
			}

			}
		}
	}

		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1151 # That's it! This ends now!
		
		piety = -10
		
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_friend = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_rival = ROOT
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			
			character_event = { id = soh.1153 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = diligent
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = humble
			}
		}
	}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1163
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								trait = envious
								trait = cruel
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Envious or Cruel and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1164 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = kind
								trait = arbitrary
							}
						}
					}

					# FROM becomes less just
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1169 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = kind
							}
							trait = wroth
						}
					}
					
					# FROM loses Wroth
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1172 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = kind
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = kind
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1174 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = kind
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1180 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = envious
								trait = cruel
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Kind
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1182 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = kind
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1184 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = kind
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1163 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1163 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

		}

			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1189
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Proud and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1190 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = humble
								trait = slothful
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes less diligent
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1194 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = humble
								trait = uncouth
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes less groomed
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1197 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = humble
								trait = proud
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is proud of not being proud
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1200 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = humble
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = humble
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1202 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = humble
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1208 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = proud
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Humble
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1210 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = humble
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1212 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = humble
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1189 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1189 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1217
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = craven
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Craven and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1218 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = brave
								trait = trusting
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more trusting
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1222 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = brave
								trait = zealous
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more zealous
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1225 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = brave
								trait = ambitious
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more ambitious
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1228 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = brave
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = brave
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1231 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = brave
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1237 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = craven
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Brave
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1239 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = brave
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1241 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = brave
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1217 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1217 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = paranoid
			}
			
			remove_trait_paranoid_effect = yes
			
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = soh.1223 } # Inform teacher
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			add_trait_trusting_effect = yes
		
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_quest = quest_hwarang_trusting
				}
				clr_quest = quest_hwarang_trusting
				add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
			}
			
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = soh.1224 } # Inform teacher
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1217 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_hwarang_brave

		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1246
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = ambitious
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Ambitious and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1247 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = content
								trait = kind
							}
							OR = {
								NOT = {
									trait = cruel
								}
								trait = envious
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes less envious
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1251 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = content
								trait = proud
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more proud
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1254 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = content
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = content
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1257 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = content
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1263 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = ambitious
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Content
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1265 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = content
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1267 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = content
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1246 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1246 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# I am Ambitious and am having second thoughts
character_event = {
	id = soh.1247
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1247
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1247 # It is for the best...
		
		piety = 10
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = diligent
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = zealous
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
				}
				
				remove_trait_ambitious_effect = yes
				
				FROM = {
					character_event = { id = soh.1248 } # Inform teacher
				}
			}
			
			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = slothful
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cynical
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 5
					trait = stubborn
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 5
					trait = proud
				}
				
				FROM = {
					character_event = { id = soh.1249 } # Inform teacher
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1246 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = patient
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1247 # No, I can't do this...
		
		piety = -10
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1250 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}
}

# If I should be Content I should not be Envious - lose Envious/become Kind
character_event = {
	id = soh.1251
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1251
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1251 # I should be less envious...
		
		piety = 10
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = envious
			}
			
			remove_trait_envious_effect = yes
			
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = soh.1252 } # Inform teacher
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			add_trait_kind_effect = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_quest = quest_hwarang_kind
				}
				clr_quest = quest_hwarang_kind
				add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
			}
			
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = soh.1253 } # Inform teacher
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1246 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1272
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = shy
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Shy and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1273 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = gregarious
								trait = cruel
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more cruel
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1277 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = gregarious
								trait = deceitful
							}
						}
					}

					# FROM becomes more deceitful
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1280 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = gregarious
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = gregarious
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1283 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = gregarious
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1289 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = shy
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Gregarious
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1291 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = gregarious
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1293 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = gregarious
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1272 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1272 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			factor = 100
			
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					trait = proud
				}
			}

				factor = 0.1
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = slothful
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}

		}
	}
}

# Teacher blames me
character_event = {
	id = soh.1286
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1286
	picture = GFX_evt_poke_king_in_chest
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1286 # Let's keep at it...
		
		prestige = -25
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1272 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					trait = proud
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = slothful
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1286 # That's it! This ends now!
		
		piety = -10
		
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_friend = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_rival = ROOT
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			
			character_event = { id = soh.1288 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = diligent
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = humble
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1291 # I'm gregarious now!
		
		add_trait_gregarious_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_quest = quest_hwarang_gregarious
			}
			clr_quest = quest_hwarang_gregarious
			add_society_currency_medium_effect = yes
		}
		
		piety = 25
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1292 } # Inform teacher!
		}
	}
}

# Inform Hwarang that they'll be taught about honesty

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1298
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = deceitful
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Deceitful and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1299 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = honest
								trait = cruel
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more cruel
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1303 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = honest
								trait = gregarious
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more gregarious
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1306 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = honest
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = honest
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1309 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = honest
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1315 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = deceitful
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Honest
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1317 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = honest
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1319 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = honest
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1298 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1298 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# I am Deceitful and am having second thoughts
character_event = {
	id = soh.1299
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1299
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1299 # It is for the best...
		
		piety = 10
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = diligent
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = zealous
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
				}
				
				remove_trait_deceitful_effect = yes
				
				FROM = {
					character_event = { id = soh.1300 } # Inform teacher
				}
			}
			
			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = slothful
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cynical
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 5
					trait = stubborn
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 5
					trait = proud
				}
				
				FROM = {
					character_event = { id = soh.1301 } # Inform teacher
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1298 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = patient
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1299 # No, I can't do this...
		
		piety = -10
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1302 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1324
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = arbitrary
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Arbitrary and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1325 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = just
								trait = cruel
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more cruel
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1329 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = just
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = just
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1332 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = just
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1338 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = arbitrary
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Just
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1340 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = just
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1342 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = just
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1324 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1324 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1347
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Paranoid and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1348 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = trusting
								trait = shy
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more shy
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1352 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = trusting
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = trusting
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1355 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = trusting
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1361 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = paranoid
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Trusting
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1363 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = trusting
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1365 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = trusting
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1347 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1347 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = soh.1370
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = cynical
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Cynical and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1371 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = zealous
								religion = ROOT
								
								# Rel heads shouldn't convert
								controls_religion = yes
								
								# Don't go unreformed
								AND = {
									korean_pagan = {
										has_flag = has_been_reformed
									}
									ROOT = {
										religion = korean_pagan
									}
								}
								
								# Remain eligible for the Hwarang
								AND = {
									NOT = {
										culture_group = koreanic
									}
									ROOT = {
										religion_openly_korean_or_reformed_trigger = no
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM has a different religion and might convert or go zealous
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1375 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = zealous
								trait = proud
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more proud
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1379 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = zealous
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = zealous
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is bad
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1382 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = zealous
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1388 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = cynical
							}
							religion = ROOT
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Zealous
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1390 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = zealous
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1392 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = zealous
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1370 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1370 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

			50 = {
				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = diligent
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = zealous
				}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
				}
				
				remove_trait_cynical_effect = yes
				
				FROM = {
