				}
			}

				mult_modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = slothful
				}

					factor = 2

				}

					trait = stubborn

					trait = proud

				trait = humble
			}

				trait = zealous

	id = soh.1379
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1379
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1379 # I should be proud of my faith!
		
		prestige = 10
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = humble
			}
			
			remove_trait_humble_effect = yes
			
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = soh.1380 } # Inform teacher
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			add_trait_proud_effect = yes
			
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = soh.1381 } # Inform teacher
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1370 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1397
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = chaste
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Chaste and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1398 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = celibate
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Celibate and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1402 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = lustful
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = chaste
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is up to no good
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1406 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = lustful
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1412 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = chaste
								trait = celibate
							}
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					# FROM becomes Lustful
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1414 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = lustful
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1416 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = lustful
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1397 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1397 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

	id = soh.1409
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1409
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1409 # Let's keep at it...
		
		prestige = -25
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1397 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					trait = paranoid
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			trait = paranoid
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1409 # You LIE!
		
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_friend = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_rival = ROOT
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			
			character_event = { id = soh.1411 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1421
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = temperate
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Temperate and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1422 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = gluttonous
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = temperate
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is up to no good
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1426 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = gluttonous
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1432 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = temperate
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Gluttonous
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1434 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = gluttonous
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1436 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = gluttonous
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1421 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1421 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1441
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = charitable
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Charitable and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1442 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = greedy
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = charitable
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is up to no good
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1446 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = greedy
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1452 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = charitable
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Greedy
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1454 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = greedy
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1456 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = greedy
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1441 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1441 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1461
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Diligent and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1462 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = slothful
								trait = content
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more content
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1466 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = greedy
								trait = patient
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more patient
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1469 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = slothful
							}
						}
					}

						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {

						}

						intrigue >= 12

						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

						intrigue >= 24
					}

						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 28

				}

							NOT = {
								trait = slothful
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1478 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Slothful
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1480 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = slothful
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1482 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = slothful
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1461 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1461 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1487
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = patient
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Patient and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1488 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = wroth
								trait = diligent
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more diligent

					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = wroth
							}
						}
					}

						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = patient
						}
					}

						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 24
					}

						intrigue >= 28
					}

					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = wroth
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1501 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = patient
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Wroth
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1503 }
				
				}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = wroth
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1505 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = wroth
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1487 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1487 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1510
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = kind
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Kind and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1511 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = envious
								trait = just
							}
						}
					}

					}
				}

					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = envious
								trait = ambitious
							}
						}
					}

					}

							NOT = {

						factor = 0.9

						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1527 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = kind
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

						learning >= 24
					}

						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Envious
					FROM = {

					}
				}

					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = envious
							}
						}
					}

						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}

					}

							NOT = {
								trait = envious
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1510 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1510 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

							}
						}
					}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1561
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = just
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Just and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1562 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = arbitrary
								trait = kind
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more kind
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1566 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = arbitrary
								trait = cynical
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more cynical
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1569 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = arbitrary
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = patient
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is up to no good
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1572 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = arbitrary
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1578 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = just
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Arbitrary
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1580 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = arbitrary
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1582 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = arbitrary
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1561 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1561 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

	id = soh.1583
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1583
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1583 # Let's keep at it...
		
		piety = 5
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1585 } # Ping student
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = wroth
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = slothful
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1583 # This won't go anywhere!
		
		prestige = -25
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1584 } # Inform student
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = patient
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = diligent
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform Hwarang the lessons ended early
character_event = {
	id = soh.1584
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1584
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1584 # I see...
		
		reverse_remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_hwarang_offering_spiritual_guidance
		}
		
		remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_hwarang_receiving_spiritual_guidance
		}
	}
}

# If the lessons didn't end early, ping the Hwarang
character_event = {
	id = soh.1585
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1561 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
	}
}



### Spiritual guidance - "bravery" (Craven)

# Inform Hwarang that they'll be taught about bravery

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1587
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = brave
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Brave and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1588 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = craven
								trait = paranoid
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more paranoid
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1592 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = craven
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = patient
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is up to no good
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1595 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = craven
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1601 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = brave
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Craven
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1603 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = craven
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1605 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = craven
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1587 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1587 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# I am Brave and really wonder why we're having this lesson
character_event = {
	id = soh.1588
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1588
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1588 # It is for the best...
		
		piety = 10
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = diligent
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = zealous
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = humble
					}
					
					remove_trait_silently_brave_effect = yes
					
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1589 } # Inform teacher
					}
				}
				
				50 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = cynical
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 5
						trait = stubborn
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 5
						trait = proud
					}
					
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1590 } # Inform teacher
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1587 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = humble
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = zealous
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = patient
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1588 # No, I can't do this...
		
		piety = -5
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1591 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = stubborn
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = proud
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = cynical
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}
}

# If I'm brave in an unsuitable way, maybe that's because I trust too much? - lose Trusting/gain Paranoid
character_event = {
	id = soh.1592
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1592
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1592 # I should be Good if I can't be Lawful!
		
		prestige = -10
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = trusting
			}
			
			remove_trait_trusting_effect = yes
			
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = soh.1593 } # Inform teacher
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_trait_paranoid_effect = yes
			
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = soh.1594 } # Inform teacher
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1587 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
	}
}

# Teacher assures me everything is okay
character_event = {
	id = soh.1598
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_1598
	picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_1598 # Let's keep at it...
		
		prestige = -25
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.1587 days = 30 random = 30 } # Back to the loop
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100

			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					trait = paranoid
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			trait = paranoid
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_1598 # You LIE!
		
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_friend = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_rival = ROOT
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_friend = ROOT
			}
			
			character_event = { id = soh.1600 } # Inform teacher
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {

			limit = {

				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = kind
						}
					}

							trait = patient
						}

						intrigue >= 12

						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					}

						intrigue >= 24
					}

						intrigue >= 28

							}

					}

							}
						}
					}

						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {

						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}

					}
				}

							NOT = {
								trait = cruel
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}

							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1610 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {

					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}

							}

					}

							trait = patient
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

						intrigue >= 24

						intrigue >= 28
					}

				}

								trait = cynical
							}
						}
					}

						factor = 0.9

					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1644 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = zealous
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Cynical
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1646 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = cynical
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1648 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = cynical
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1630 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1630 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1653
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							trait = honest
						}
					}
					
					# FROM is Honest and might reconsider lessons
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1654 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = deceitful
								trait = paranoid
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more paranoid
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1658 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = deceitful
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							trait = paranoid
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						NOT = {
							trait = patient
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						is_dumb_trigger = yes
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.8
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM thinks their teacher is up to no good
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1661 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = deceitful
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1667 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = honest
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM becomes Deceitful
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1669 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = deceitful
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1671 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = deceitful
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1653 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1653 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

# Looping progress event
character_event = {
	id = soh.1676
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					society_member_of = hwarang
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				# No "Hey, I've already got the trait; why am I doing this again?" here; you're Trusting, and thus gullible!
				# Also no "Hey; my teacher seems to be trying to do the opposite of their stated goal!"; if you notice it, they've succeeded!
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = paranoid
								trait = cynical
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM becomes more cynical
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1677 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								trait = trusting
								trait = paranoid
							}
							any_friend = {
								NOT = {
									character = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					# FROM ends a friendship
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1680 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = paranoid
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.9
						diplomacy >= 28
					}
					
					# FROM is having doubts
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1683 }
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						FROM = {
							NOR = {
								any_friend = {
									NOT = {
										character = ROOT
									}
								}
								any_lover = {
									NOT = {
										character = ROOT
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						FROM = {
							trait = trusting
						}
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.05
						learning >= 28
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 12
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 16
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 20
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 24
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						intrigue >= 28
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							trait = trusting
						}
						
						remove_trait_silently_trusting_effect = yes
						
						repeat_event = { id = soh.1676 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
					}
					
					else = {
						# FROM becomes Paranoid
						FROM = {
							character_event = { id = soh.1685 }
						}
					}
				}
				
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = paranoid
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = slothful
					}

					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						FROM = {
							trait = slothful
						}
					}
					
					# Teacher might think it is going nowhere
					FROM = {
						character_event = { id = soh.1687 }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					trigger = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								trait = paranoid
							}
						}
					}
					
					# Nothing - loop back!
					repeat_event = { id = soh.1676 days = 30 random = 30 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_alive = yes
					society_member_of = hwarang
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.1676 days = 30 random = 30 } # Try again
		}
	}
}

			limit = {

				FROM = {
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					trigger = {

							trait = gregarious
						}
					}

				factor = 0.1

			}

				factor = 0.1
				trait = slothful
			}

				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}

		}
